NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
I, P. Ganapathy, born as male child to R. Perumal on 5-3-1977 have been residing at Orathur Village, Nathamedu,
Villupuram-605 601. After the Biological change a Sex reassignment Surgery was performed from Male to Femal and has
been living as a female. [Reference: Dr. Sak Meeran, M.B.B.S. M.S., GENMAC., DAC (CEYLON) No. 3, North Kaliamman
Koil Street, Dindukal.] The clinical examination under the reference above also show that, I could live as a female. Hence,
I, P. Ganapathy shall henceforth be known as P. MANJU.

Villupuram,
21st September 2015.

P. GANAPATHY.
